          <p class="break-words text-color-text" data-test-id="about-us__description">
              Mplus is a European leader in business process and technology outsourcing (BPTO). It operates as part of the BOSQAR INVEST group, serving as its BPTO vertical, which includes the parent company, M Plus Croatia d.o.o, along with its subsidiaries.

Mplus successfully integrates the dynamic industries of contact centers, information technology, and employment services to address global challenges in customer support. Through its innovative business model, Mplus has built a diverse portfolio of clients, including leading European and global telecommunications, financial, technology, energy, logistics, and consumer goods companies.

With operational centers across 42 sites in 13 countries, the Mplus community comprises over 12,800 employees who deliver top-notch customer experiences in over 32 languages.

In addition to its presence in Croatia, Mplus operates in markets including Bosnia and Herzegovina, Georgia, Germany, Hungary, Romania, Serbia, Slovakia, Slovenia, Spain, Turkey, the UK, and the USA.

Mplus has an in-house technology division, which brings together the tech companies within the BPTO group. Their wide range of products, services, and consulting solutions is carefully designed to transform how companies interact with their customers and manage their processes, offering cutting-edge tools to enhance customer experience, optimize operations, and embrace digital¬†transformation.

    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">üèÜWe came back from Rovinj with four HR awards!

Mplus has been recognized as a Top Workplace on a group level (12,500+ employees) and received the Best of the Best Award in several Mplus companies in the region: <a class="link" href="https://si.linkedin.com/company/mpluslovenia?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Mplus Slovenia</a>, <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/company/mplusbosniaherzegovina?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Mplus Bosnia &amp; Herzegovina</a>, and <a class="link" href="https://rs.linkedin.com/company/mpluserbia?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Mplus Serbia</a>!

These awards, presented by <a class="link" href="https://hr.linkedin.com/company/luppa-app?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Luppa</a>, were announced during this year‚Äôs <a class="link" href="https://hr.linkedin.com/company/hr-weekend?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>HR.WEEKEND</a>, a perfect setting to celebrate our shared achievements.

Here‚Äôs what makes it special:

‚Ä¢	Top Workplace goes to companies scoring at least 15% above industry benchmarks in engagement, satisfaction, eNPS, and Luppa‚Äôs 12 dimensions.
‚Ä¢	Best of the Best celebrates organizations that exceed both benchmarks by 25% or more and rank among the top three in their market and size category - true leaders in creating exceptional workplaces.

"These awards are more than recognition¬†- they‚Äôre a reflection of real feedback and the daily effort of our people: management, HR, and employees alike. Thanks to Luppa, we now have deeper insights than ever to turn feedback into meaningful action. At Mplus, people inspire people, and that‚Äôs what these awards celebrate!", <a class="link" href="https://hr.linkedin.com/in/bruna-kostelac-ko%C5%A1ir-9b31582?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Bruna Kostelac Ko≈°ir</a>, Chief People Officer at Mplus said.

A huge thank you to everyone who contributes to making Mplus a great place to work!¬†

  <div class="attributed-text-segment-list__container relative mt-1 mb-1.5 babybear:mt-0 babybear:mb-0.5">
    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">At this year‚Äôs <a class="link" href="https://hr.linkedin.com/company/weekend-media-festival?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Weekend Media Festival</a> in Rovinj, Mplus's Chief People Officer, <a class="link" href="https://hr.linkedin.com/in/bruna-kostelac-ko%C5%A1ir-9b31582?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Bruna Kostelac Ko≈°ir</a>, moderated the panel, "It‚Äôs a Kind of Magic! When HR Drives the ESG Agenda". She was joined on stage by <a class="link" href="https://hr.linkedin.com/in/lucia-ana-tomi%C4%87-57b0869?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Lucia Ana Tomiƒá</a> (<a class="link" href="https://hr.linkedin.com/company/wiener-osiguranje-vienna-insurance-group-d.d.?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Wiener osiguranje Vienna Insurance Group d.d.</a> ) and <a class="link" href="https://hr.linkedin.com/in/hana-hrpka-74908855?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Hana Hrpka</a> (<a class="link" href="https://hr.linkedin.com/company/hrabri-telefon?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Hrabri telefon (Brave phone)</a>).

The discussion highlighted a crucial point: people bring ESG strategies to life. Panelists agreed that HR‚Äôs role is expanding ‚Äì proactive leadership is essential. ESG strategies can only succeed when HR steps up and takes responsibility, rather than playing the ‚Äúnot my job‚Äù card.

As Bruna concluded: ‚ÄúIf you want to be truly strategic, start with your core business ‚Äì identify what you do best and which NGO you can support most effectively. That‚Äôs how real partnerships are built.‚Äù

For more insights from the panel, see the full announcement here: <a class="link" href="http://tinyurl.com/5n8wduj9?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" rel="nofollow" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>tinyurl.com/5n8wduj9</a>

    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">ESG has made its way to boardroom agendas. But what happens when HR turns strategies into real impact?

Mplus's Chief People Officer, <a class="link" href="https://hr.linkedin.com/in/bruna-kostelac-ko%C5%A1ir-9b31582?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Bruna Kostelac Ko≈°ir</a>, will take on that very question as the moderator of a panel bringing together two powerful perspectives:

üî∏ <a class="link" href="https://hr.linkedin.com/in/lucia-ana-tomi%C4%87-57b0869?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Lucia Ana Tomiƒá</a> ‚Äì Head of HR and Regulatory Affairs, <a class="link" href="https://hr.linkedin.com/company/wiener-osiguranje-vienna-insurance-group-d.d.?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Wiener osiguranje Vienna Insurance Group d.d.</a>
üî∏ <a class="link" href="https://hr.linkedin.com/in/hana-hrpka-74908855?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Hana Hrpka</a> ‚Äì Executive Director &amp; President, <a class="link" href="https://hr.linkedin.com/company/hrabri-telefon?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Hrabri telefon (Brave phone)</a>

The conversation will cut through theory and dive into:

‚ú® how talent and culture can push and co-create ESG strategy,
‚ú® how HR can measure the impact of ESG,
‚ú® and what it looks like when change reaches beyond business and into community.

Not a buzzword session. A real look at what happens when HR leads on ESG.

üëâ Don‚Äôt miss it. See you at the <a class="link" href="https://hr.linkedin.com/company/hr-weekend?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>HR.WEEKEND</a> in Rovinj!

        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">Exciting news! Mplus has been shortlisted for nine categories at the prestigious 2025 A.I. Awards, a global program celebrating the brightest innovations in artificial intelligence.

The group has been shortlisted in the following categories:

 üîπ Best Use of AI in Transportation &amp; Logistics
 üîπ AI Deployment of the Year
 üîπ Best AI-driven Automation Solution
 üîπ Best Use of AI in Natural Language Processing (NLP) and Translation
 üîπ Most Advanced AI Environment
 üîπ Best Use of AI in Customer Service
 üîπ Best Use of AI in Telecoms / Unified Communications / Conferencing
 üîπ Best Use of AI in Retail &amp; eCommerce
 üîπ Best Use of AI-driven Personalization

The recognition places Mplus alongside leading international technology players such as IBM, Cognizant, Genesys, Capital One, DeepL, Bloomreach, and Talkdesk. 

‚ÄúMplus‚Äôs multi-category recognition at the A.I. Awards is a testament to our commitment to delivering practical, impactful AI solutions that enhance customer experiences and operational efficiency across industries,‚Äù said <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/in/kodaskurzewski?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Koda Skurzewski (Sker - je - ski ), OMCP</a>, Board Member and Chief Commercial Officer at Mplus. 

‚ÄúTo be recognized alongside some of the world‚Äôs most influential AI innovators is both an honor and a motivator as we continue to invest in next-generation technologies,‚Äù she added.

Winners will be announced in October 2025, with honorees selected from across the US, Canada, Europe, Asia, and Australia.

    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">
As part of the first Mplus Culture Week, employees across nine countries took part in the Move &amp; Groove Challenge, a global step competition promoting wellness, motivation, and team spirit.¬†
¬†
Over just five days, participants achieved incredible results: 

14,957,032 steps ‚Äì covering 11,218 km, nearly a quarter of Earth‚Äôs circumference üåç¬†
¬†
54,787 steps per participant on average ‚Äì roughly a marathon üèÉ‚ôÄ¬†
¬†
Team Winner: üá∏üáÆ Slovenia ‚Äì 92,327 steps ‚åö¬†
¬†
Individual Winner: üá∑üá∏ Serbia ‚Äì 330,268 steps üèÜ ‚Äì close to the distance from Zagreb to Madrid!¬†
¬†
The Move &amp; Groove Challenge proved that every step counts ‚Äì and when we move together, we can achieve amazing things. üí™üëü¬†
¬†
